    gotoLabelRequests: s32'landing'

    endIf:

      velocityXRate: 50
    endIf: 
  endUpon:

beginSubroutine: s32'usg_CheckEnemyName'
  returnValue: 0, 0
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'kyk'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    returnValue: 0, 1
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'ask'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    returnValue: 0, 1
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'ven'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    returnValue: 0, 1
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'sin'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    returnValue: 0, 1
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginState: s32'CmnActMatchWin'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnactmatchwin'
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 2147483647
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(0)
      createObject: s32'800cs_rabbit', (PLAYER)
      createObject: s32'800cs_tools', (PLAYER)
      ifTrueInObject: (To3_ENEMY_MAIN_PLAYER), Mem(CmnCharaReg22)
        runOnObject: (To3_ENEMY_MAIN_PLAYER)
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg22), Val(4)
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(1)
      playAnimation: s32'usg800cs', 0
      checkLastStateName: s32'WinActionWait'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        playCameraAnimation: s32'usg800cs', 23, 0, -1
      endIf: 
      else: 
        playCameraAnimation: s32'usg800cs', 23, 0, -1
      endElse: 
      cinesco: 1
      swapMeshSet: s32'800cs'
      resetSaturation: 1, 1
      setPostProcessSaturation: -1, 800, 50
      resetDiffusion: 1, 1
      setDiffusionLuminance: -1, 1400, 50
      setDiffusionThreshold: -1, 0, 50
      hideAllButSelf: 1
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(2)
      characterSfx: s32'SE_BTL_USG_MatchWin_00'
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(20)
      resetDOF: 1, 1
      focalDistance: -1, 700, 0
      focalRegion: -1, 0, 0
      focalNearTransition: -1, 0, 0

beginSubroutine: s32'USG_ThrowCheck'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(3)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      setDepth: -60000
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(5)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      setDepth: -20000
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(6)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      setDepth: -40000
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
      exPointFReset: (PLAYER), 140000, 360000
      setGripPosition: (EX_POINT_F), (NECK), 0
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
      exPointFReset: (PLAYER), 140000, 360000
      setGripPosition: (EX_POINT_F), (NECK), 0
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(7)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      setDepth: -60000
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(8)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      setDepth: -30000
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(11)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
